<dsc reserve="519" >/**
 * BusinessDelegate is an implementation of the &lt;i&gt;Business Delegate&lt;/i&gt; pattern.
 * The &lt;i&gt;Business Delegate&lt;/i&gt; encapsulates the logic and implementation of locating
 * and executing business services. The &lt;i&gt;Business Delegate&lt;/i&gt; uses a &lt;i&gt;Service Locator&lt;/i&gt;
 * to lookup the remote &lt;i&gt;Business Facade&lt;/i&gt;, and delegates the control of businesss processing 
 * to the &lt;i&gt;Business Facade&lt;/i&gt;.
 * 
 * @author person7553f5959484
 * @version $Revision: 1.4 $ $Author: psa2920 $ $Date: 2004/06/17 14:49:12 $
 */</dsc>
<nam>BusinessDelegate</nam>

<dsc reserve="636" >/**
 * Initializes this filter before processing can start. If a sub class needs
 * additional initialization, it should override the {@link #doInit()} method.
 * &lt;p/&gt;
 * This is a template method that performs the following ordered steps:
 * &lt;ol&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; logs that initialization started &lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; assigns the FilterConfig to the protected {@link #filterConfig} variable &lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; calls the protected {@link #doInit()} method that may be overridden by the sub class&lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; logs that initialization ended &lt;/li&gt;
 * &lt;/ol&gt;
 * 
 * @inheritDoc
 * @see javax.servlet.Filter#init(javax.servlet.FilterConfig)
 */</dsc>
<nam>init</nam>
<isl>TRUE</isl>

 * 	&lt;li&gt; logs that initialization started &lt;/li&gt;

 * 	&lt;li&gt; calls the protected {@link #doInit()} method that may be overridden by the sub class&lt;/li&gt;

<dsc reserve="758" >/**
 * Convenient method called by {@link #doFilter(javax.servlet.ServletRequest, javax.servlet.ServletResponse, javax.servlet.FilterChain)},

 *

<dsc reserve="492" >/**
 * Destroys the filter. If a sub class needs
 * additional initialization, it should override the {@link #doDestroy()} method.
 * &lt;p/&gt;
 * This is a template method that performs the following ordered steps:
 * &lt;ol&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; logs that destruction started &lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; calls the protected {@link #doDestroy()} method that may be overridden by the sub class&lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; logs that destruction ended &lt;/li&gt;
 * &lt;/ol&gt;
 * 
 * @inheritDoc
 * @see javax.servlet.Filter#destroy()

<dsc reserve="740" >/**
 * Performs the following processing steps:
 * &lt;ol&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; Loads TransactionContext from Session if possible &lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; Updates TransactionContext with current screenId &lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; Updates TransactionContext with current processId &lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; Updates TransactionContext with current transactionId &lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; Delegates processing to the next filter or resource in the chain &lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; Stores TransactionContext in Session if possible &lt;/li&gt;
 * 	&lt;li&gt; Resets TransactionContext before next time&lt;/li&gt;
 * &lt;/ol&gt;
 * 
 * @inheritDoc
 * @see no.trygdeetaten.web.framework.filter.AbstractFilter#doFilter(javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest, javax.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse, javax.servlet.FilterChain)
 */</dsc>
